    200:     private static boolean subscriberCanRead(Roles roles, RelationName relationName, Role subscriber, String publicationName) {
    201:         boolean canRead = roles.hasPrivilege(subscriber, Permission.DQL, Securable.TABLE, relationName.fqn());
    202:         if (canRead == false) {
    203:             if (LOGGER.isInfoEnabled()) {
    204:                 LOGGER.info("User {} subscribed to the publication {} doesn't have DQL privilege on the table {}, this table will not be replicated.",

    206:             }
    207:         }
    208:         return canRead;
    209:     }

    396:     private static Set<RelationName> getExistingLocallyTables(Subscription subscription,
    397:                                                                ClusterState subscriberClusterState,
    398:                                                                Response publisherStateResponse) {
    399:         // Table existence check is done on a subscription creation but
    400:         // there are cases when attempt to subscribe to existing table happens later during the replication.

    416:             }

<thinking>Root cause is that the method getState() is called on objects in LogicalReplicationRepository.java but is not found in Publication.java, indicating API drift where getState() is expected on a response type in LogicalReplicationRepository but not in Publication. Also, the Predicate import and usage in Publication.java is correct and present.     185:     @VisibleForTesting
    186:     public static Function<IndexMetadata, IndexMetadata> applyCustomIndexSettings(ClusterState state) {
    187:         // mark indices where not all shards are active yet, restore will fail if primaries are not (yet) assigned
    188:         return im -> {
    189:             var routingTable = state.routingTable().index(im.getIndex());
    190:             assert routingTable != null : "routingTable must not be null";
    191:             boolean isActive = routingTable.allPrimaryShardsActive();
    192:             IndexMetadata.Builder builder = IndexMetadata.builder(im);
    193:             return builder.settings(Settings.builder()
    194:                     .put(im.getSettings())
    195:                     .put(REPLICATION_INDEX_ROUTING_ACTIVE.getKey(), isActive))
    196:                 .build();
    197:         };
    198:     }

 >  200:     private static boolean subscriberCanRead(Roles roles, RelationName relationName, Role subscriber, String publicationName) {
    201:         boolean canRead = roles.hasPrivilege(subscriber, Permission.DQL, Securable.TABLE, relationName.fqn());
    202:         if (canRead == false) {
    203:             if (LOGGER.isInfoEnabled()) {
    204:                 LOGGER.info("User {} subscribed to the publication {} doesn't have DQL privilege on the table {}, this table will not be replicated.",
    205:                     subscriber.name(), publicationName, relationName.fqn());
    206:             }
    207:         }
    208:         return canRead;
    209:     }

+    public static Function<IndexMetadata, IndexMetadata> applyCustomIndexSettings(ClusterState state) {
+        // mark indices where not all shards are active yet, restore will fail if primaries are not (yet) assigned
+        return im -> {

 >  200:     private static boolean subscriberCanRead(Roles roles, RelationName relationName, Role subscriber, String publicationName) {
